54_CD Summary_NNP and_CC Conclusions_NNP ._.
1_CD ._.
The_DT blood-sucking_JJ Muscidæ_NNP are_VBP descended_VBN from_IN a_DT Musca-like_JJ ancestor_NN ._.
The_DT entomological_JJ facts_NNS make_VBP it_PRP improbable_JJ that_IN the_DT flagellates_NNS found_VBN in_IN the_DT alimentary_JJ tract_NN of_IN blood-sucking_JJ flies_NNS ,_, and_CC of_IN non-blood_NN suckers_NNS which_WDT are_VBP allied_VBN to_TO them_PRP ,_, are_VBP derived_VBN from_IN the_DT parasites_NNS in_IN vertebrate_NN blood_NN ._.

2_CD ._.

3_CD ._.
In_IN the_DT genus_NN Philæmatomyia_NNP there_EX are_VBP three_CD species_NNS which_WDT show_VBP separate_JJ steps_NNS in_IN the_DT modification_NN of_IN the_DT Musca-like_NNP proboscis_NN to_TO a_DT biting_NN apparatus_NN ._.

They_PRP are:55_VBP a_DT membraneous_JJ interval_NN left_VBD in_IN the_DT region_NN of_IN the_DT joint_JJ which_WDT permits_VBZ the_DT furca_NN to_TO be_VB rotated_VBN freely_RB backwards_NNS ._.
6_CD ._.
In_IN all_PDT the_DT flies_NNS dealt_VBP with_IN ,_, in_IN the_DT order_NN given_VBN ,_, there_EX is_VBZ an_DT increase_NN in_IN the_DT relative_JJ length_NN of_IN the_DT haustellum_NN ,_, and_CC a_DT diminution_NN in_IN that_DT of_IN the_DT rostrum_NN ,_, together_RB with_IN some_DT diminution_NN in_IN the_DT amount_NN of_IN movement_NN between_IN the_DT latter_NN and_CC the_DT head_NN capsule_NN ._.
7_CD ._.
Glossina_NNP represents_VBZ an_DT extreme_JJ case_NN ,_, and_CC there_EX is_VBZ a_DT wide_JJ interval_NN between_IN it_PRP and_CC the_DT Stomoxydinæ_NNP ._.
